THREAD-SAFETY PATTERNS IN CODEBASE\n\nThe codebase uses consistent patterns for thread-safe implementations:\n\n#### **Pattern A: sync.RWMutex for Read-Heavy Operations**\n\n**File:** `/workspace/internal/storage/fs/cache.go` (Lines 28-194)\n\n```go\ntype SnapshotCache[K comparable] struct {\n    mu sync.RWMutex\n\n    logger *zap.Logger\n\n    fixed map[string]K\n    extra *lru.Cache[string, K]\n\n    store map[K]*Snapshot\n}\n\n// Read operation with RLock\nfunc (c *SnapshotCache[K]) Get(ref string) (s *Snapshot, ok bool) {\n    c.mu.RLock()\n    defer c.mu.RUnlock()\n\n    k, ok := c.fixed[ref]\n    if ok {\n        s, ok = c.store[k]\n        return\n    }\n\n    k, ok = c.extra.Get(ref)\n    if !ok {\n        return s, ok\n    }\n\n    s, ok = c.store[k]\n    return\n}\n\n// Write operation with Lock\nfunc (c *SnapshotCache[K]) AddOrBuild(ctx context.Context, ref string, k K, build CacheBuildFunc[K]) (s *Snapshot, err error) {\n    s, ok := c.getByRefAndKey(ref, k)\n    if ok {\n        return s, nil\n    }\n\n    if s == nil {\n        s, err = build(ctx, k)\n        if err != nil {\n            return s, err\n        }\n    }\n\n    c.mu.Lock()\n    defer c.mu.Unlock()\n    \n    // Update operations...\n    c.store[k] = s\n    return s, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### **Pattern B: sync.Mutex for Simple Exclusive Access**\n\n**File:** While the codebase already tracks metrics via OpenTelemetry (OTEL) histogram, we need a separate internal duration tracking component that provides aggregate statistics (count, average, P99 latency) for the evaluation engine. This will enable SLO setting and performance regression detection.\n\n## Current State\n- Evaluation metrics already exist: `metrics.EvaluationLatency` (OTEL Histogram) at `/workspace/internal/server/metrics/metrics.go`\n- Three evaluation methods in `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n  - `Variant()` - Evaluates multi-variate flags\n  - `Boolean()` - Evaluates boolean flags (already has latency recording)\n  - `Batch()` - Batch evaluation of multiple flags\n- Thread-safety patterns in codebase use `sync.Mutex` or `sync.RWMutex` with defer-based lock management\n\n## Implementation Approach\n\n### 1.
